## Project Structure

```sh
└── ife-hospital.git/
    ├── README.md
    ├── database
    │   └── teleclinic.sql
    ├── environment
    │   └── apache2
    ├── recording
    │   ├── .htaccess
    │   ├── application
    │   ├── batch.php
    │   ├── config.inc
    │   ├── core
    │   ├── data
    │   ├── index.php
    │   ├── log
    │   ├── readme.md
    │   └── resource
    ├── scs
    │   ├── Gruntfile.js
    │   ├── api.js
    │   ├── config.js
    │   ├── db.js
    │   ├── errors.js
    │   ├── package.json
    │   ├── server.js
    │   ├── server.min.js
    │   ├── service
    │   └── ssl
    ├── turn
    │   ├── account.txt
    │   ├── libevent-2.1.8-stable.tar.gz
    │   └── turnserver-4.5.0.7.tar.gz
    └── www
        ├── .htaccess
        ├── .jshintrc
        ├── Gruntfile.js
        ├── application
        ├── batch.php
        ├── config.inc
        ├── core
        ├── data
        ├── index.php
        ├── lang.php
        ├── log
        ├── package.json
        ├── plugins
        ├── readme.md
        ├── resource
        └── watch_sass.cmd
```

## Getting Started

### Prerequisites

This project requires the following dependencies:

- **Programming Language:** PHP
- **Package Manager:** Npm, Composer, Bower

### Installation

Build ife-hospital.git from the source and intsall dependencies:

1. **Clone the repository:**

    ```sh
    ❯ git clone https://github.com/Markcus0526/ife-hospital.git
    ```

2. **Navigate to the project directory:**

    ```sh
    ❯ cd ife-hospital.git
    ```

---

## Contributing

- **💬 [Join the Discussions](https://github.com/Markcus0526/ife-hospital.git/discussions)**: Share your insights, provide feedback, or ask questions.
- **🐛 [Report Issues](https://github.com/Markcus0526/ife-hospital.git/issues)**: Submit bugs found or log feature requests for the `ife-hospital.git` project.
- **💡 [Submit Pull Requests](https://github.com/Markcus0526/ife-hospital.git/blob/main/CONTRIBUTING.md)**: Review open PRs, and submit your own PRs.

<details closed>
<summary>Contributing Guidelines</summary>

1. **Fork the Repository**: Start by forking the project repository to your github account.
2. **Clone Locally**: Clone the forked repository to your local machine using a git client.
   ```sh
   git clone https://github.com/Markcus0526/ife-hospital.git
   ```
3. **Create a New Branch**: Always work on a new branch, giving it a descriptive name.
   ```sh
   git checkout -b new-feature-x
   ```
4. **Make Your Changes**: Develop and test your changes locally.
5. **Commit Your Changes**: Commit with a clear message describing your updates.
   ```sh
   git commit -m 'Implemented new feature x.'
   ```
6. **Push to github**: Push the changes to your forked repository.
   ```sh
   git push origin new-feature-x
   ```
7. **Submit a Pull Request**: Create a PR against the original project repository. Clearly describe the changes and their motivations.
8. **Review**: Once your PR is reviewed and approved, it will be merged into the main branch. Congratulations on your contribution!
</details>

<details closed>
